[1;38;5;160m|[m * [33mcommit 8207dba[m
[1;38;5;160m|[m[1;38;5;160m/[m  Author: deepsource-autofix[bot] <62050782+deepsource-autofix[bot]@users.noreply.github.com>
[1;38;5;160m|[m   Date:   9 months ago
[1;38;5;160m|[m   
[1;38;5;160m|[m       refactor: refactor unnecessary `else` / `elif` when `if` block has a `return` statement
[1;38;5;160m|[m       
[1;38;5;160m|[m       The use of `else` or `elif` becomes redundant and can be dropped if the last statement under the leading `if` / `elif` block is a `return` statement.
[1;38;5;160m|[m       In the case of an `elif` after `return`, it can be written as a separate `if` block.
[1;38;5;160m|[m       For `else` blocks after `return`, the statements can be shifted out of `else`. Please refer to the examples below for reference.
[1;38;5;160m|[m       
[1;38;5;160m|[m       Refactoring the code this way can improve code-readability and make it easier to maintain.
[1;38;5;160m|[m
